Experience Draft Champions, an all-new, fast-paced way to play online where you\'ll draft your fantasy team of NFL superstars and legends, then take them to the field to battle it out against the computer or in head to head matchups. All-new QB controls including body-relative throws, plus enhanced touch and roll out passes provide you with unprecedented depth and control while under center. Combined with a new risk/reward catch and pass-defend system, get ready for the biggest WOW moments in franchise history. </p>\n<h3>An All New Way To Play</h3>\n<h4>LIKE FANTASY FOOTBALL? THEN YOU\'LL LOVE DRAFT CHAMPIONS.</h4>\n<p>Get all of the excitement that comes with drafting a fantasy team and competing in Madden with our newest game mode: Draft Champions. First, you\'re the general manager, building your team through the draft. Then, take your team to the gridiron for a few fast-paced games of Madden football.</p>\n<h4>DRAFT YOUR TEAM IN MINUTES</h4>\n<p>No need to prepare for this draft. After selecting one of three coaches, you\'re shown three players to choose from in each round. Pick your favorite players, your hometown team, a position you need, or just go with the numbers. Any of these players will improve your starter team.</p>\n<p>Do you take a quarterback right away, or choose a linebacker now and gamble on finding a signal-caller later? Choose from current NFL superstars and legends from the past. The draft is 15 quick rounds that you can complete in a few minutes.</p>\n<h4>PLAY QUICK GAMES</h4>\n<p>Now take the team you\'ve created and hit the gridiron for a few quick games of Madden NFL 16 football. Each game has speedy three-minute quarters and takes about 15 minutes. Get the real NFL experience from the new and improved Madden NFL 16, the best-reviewed NFL video game in years.</p>\n<h4>WIN MUT REWARDS</h4>\n<p>Victory earns you bragging rights and a special pack of items you can use in Madden Ultimate Team, the fastest-growing mode in Madden NFL 16. Madden Ultimate Team (MUT) is the complete NFL team-building mode. When you begin your MUT team, the Draft Champions rewards you\'ve earned will give you a head start on other players.</p>\n<p>Draft Champions is like NFL fantasy football, but you get to play the games.</p>\n<div class="extra_content_gameinformer_preview" style="border-style: solid; border-color: #00659f; border-width:3px; border-radius: 0px; background-color: rgb(236, 236, 236); margin-bottom:2%;">\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/gameinformer/site-logo_beta.png" style="width:50%; display: block; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; padding-top: 2%;">\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/gameinformer/testchamber_hub_logo_v3.jpg" style="width:60%; display: block; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; padding-bottom:2%;">\n<h4>Test Chamber  -  Madden NFL 16</h4>\n<h5>by Matthew Kato</h5>\n<p style="padding-top:2%; font-size:1.4em; text-align: center;">Pre-season in the NFL is normally a love/hate thing as you\'re glad football is back, but hate the prospect of waiting through a month of meaningless games. What else do you need to know? Well, here are ten very excellent reasons why you and all your friends should play Madden NFL 16!</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons1.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#1: On Offense</h4>\n<p>Air Supremacy revolutionizes passing and catching on both sides of the ball with new user and AI mechanics. There is also a new multiplayer catch interaction system with more than 400 new two-player catch animations with a wide variety of outcomes.  </p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons2.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#2: On Defense</h4>\n<p>Forget everything you remember about Pro-Tak. Madden NFL 16 delivers the most dramatic tackles in franchise history with a fully organic, physics-based gang tackling system. We now have fully-realized momentum-based organic interactions on tackles that support a limitless number of defenders attaching to the ball carrier.</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons3.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#3: Beyond Broadcast</h4>\n<p>Madden NFL 16 is the second year the franchise has leveraged the experience of Brian Murray, former  NFL Films Cinematographer, in presentation. This year, the team wanted to continue to push the envelope and go beyond what normal broadcasts are able to do.</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons4.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#4: In The Franchise</h4>\n<p>Everything in Connected Franchise is done thinking about our players first, and all these new features came directly from community feedback and play-test sessions. We\'re committed to making an easy-to-use, deep Connected Franchise Mode that hits on all the features you crave. </p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons5.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#5: On Draft Day</h4>\n<p>Draft Champions adds to the Fantasy Football experience by paying off draft night immediately. As soon as the draft is over, players can take the new squad onto the field. It combines the best parts of Fantasy Football with an exciting Madden event that can be completed in an evening.</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons6.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#6: Master Your Game</h4>\n<p>Returning to Madden NFL 16 is Skills Trainer, a mode that teaches players new game mechanics and basic Madden NFL skills. Madden NFL 16 builds on this foundation by bringing up the total content to more than 60 tutorials and drills, including a brand new set of tutorials. </p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons7.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#7: With Real Life Ratings</h4>\n<p>Check out all your favorite players and stay connected to the real-world NFL with the Madden Ratings Hub, updated throughout the 2015-16 NFL season. Check back all season long as more Madden 16 player ratings are added.</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons8.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#8:With Your Ultimate Team</h4>\n<p>For the first time this year in Madden Ultimate Team (MUT), players will experience Ultimate Moments. These special Solo Challenges feature exciting, game-changing turning points taken from actual NFL game situations.</p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons9.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#9: Listen to EA Trax</h4>\n<p>Madden NFL 16 marks the return of the legendary EA Trax soundtrack, recognized as the industry\'s foremost music showcase. The Madden NFL 16 soundtrack features more than 30 tracks from artists you already know and love, </p>\n<img src="http://www.gamestop.com/gs/images/content-pdp/MaddenNFL16/Top10Reasons10.jpg" style="padding-top:2%;">\n<h4>#10: The Most Realistic Madden Ever</h4>\n<p>Madden NFL 16 includes added logic for QBs, RBs, WRs and defenders so that each head and eye track (the ball and players around them) uniquely based on their position. This year, we made huge strides in pre, post and during play motion quality. When it comes to in-game animation quality improvements, the list is endless.</p>\n<h3>KEY FEATURES:</h3>\n<h4>New to Madden</h4>\n<h5>Battle for Air Supremacy</h5>\n<ul>\n<li>Total Control Passing  -  Place the ball where only your receiver can get it with body-relative throws including high-point, low-point, and the ever popular touch pass.  Become the ultimate dual-threat and terrorize defenses with new pressure avoidance and QB scramble controls.\n<li>Receiver/Defender Controls  -  Dictate the outcome of each passing play while the ball is in the air for the first time ever in Madden. For receivers, go for the highlight reel with the aggressive\' catch or move the chains with the possession\' catch.  On defense, disrupt the outcome of each play using the new play ball\' and hit receiver\' mechanics. Receivers and defenders deliver the most authentic exchanges to date with new press and zone-chuck interactions, contextual hand-fighting, and a variety of 2-man interactions at the catch point including pass interference penalties, tip balls, knock outs and simultaneous possession catches.\n</li></li></ul>\n<h5>Playmaker Broadcast</h5>\n<ul>\n<li>Integrated Broadcast Graphics  -  Your playmaker highlight reel has arrived with new player spotlights, dynamic goals and achievements, and innovative on-the-field cameras bringing you closer to the game than ever before. Making plays has never been this much fun and rewarding! \n</li></ul>\n<h4>A New Way To Play</h4>\n<ul><li>Draft Champions - Draft your fantasy team of NFL superstars and legends and prove your superiority in this new and fastpaced way to play Madden. Whether you\'re playing solo or head-to-head campaigns, every decision matters from the moment you\'re on the clock to the final play in your undefeated run. Once you\'ve completed your campaign, implement your new strategy and begin your next Draft Championship.</li></ul>\n<h4>Playmaker Soundtrack</h4>\n<ul><li>EA Trax  -  Celebrate your playmaker journey in style with the return of licensed music in Madden, complete with 30+ new tracks featured in-stadium and in menus.</li></ul>\n<h4>Game Modes</h4>\n<ul>\n<li>Connected Franchise  -  Whether playing solo or online with friends, your quest to build an NFL dynasty begins with Connected Franchise. Interact and build your team with more control with Game Prep. Want to develop your backup QB? Between matchups, spend extra time on him each week to earn training points without having to force him into the real games before he is ready. Build your teams\' confidence through performance and front office transactions. Balance keeping player\'s confidence up, to increase abilities and build player XP.\n<li>Madden Ultimate Team  -  Build your ultimate team with your favorite NFL players from the past and present while dominating the opposition in head-to-head seasons, solo challenges, and more. Earn coins to buy packs through the online store, where you can trade and auction off items on the road to building the Ultimate Team. Engage with the NFL year round thanks to live content and service updates in the fastest growing mode in Madden.\n<li>Skills Trainer  -  With 60+ tutorials and drills, Skills Trainer focuses on teaching the strategy behind different passing and run concepts, as well as how to play Madden for new users to the series. Fan favorite Gauntlet mode returns with all-new Boss Battles, Extra Life challenges, and opportunities to jump or fall levels in a single itemprop="description"> Going into Madden 16 after owning Madden 15 was kind of a risky move on my part being as 15 lacked almost everything we were expecting (besides the huge next gen graphic update) I gave EA another chance and searched store to store for the Deluxe edition. Starting up the game, they have re-introduced the soundtracks as the old maddens used to own to themselves. The one thing I did not like, as being a die hard New England fan, is that their opening gameplay started with Superbowl 50 as the Steelers vs the Cardinals? Every single Madden be it last year had the super bowl champions somewhere showcased on the game. It always seems to be that Madden has something against that specific team and always leaves them left out. But besides that, Ultimate team and Draft Champions are the best 2 game modes the game owns to itself. Opening packs and unlocking new players in Ultimate has never felt better, they stepped up the pack opening animations and really added intensity to the feel whenever you get yourself a good card. It has a great server that matches you with people of your skill level and your team overall so that you wont get stuck against someone who has a huge advantage over you. Ive already put over 80+ hours into Ultimate team alone, and with those 80 hours alone, I can say the game lived up to its price already.\n</span> 9/15/15\n<meta content="2015-09-15" itemprop="datePublished"/>\n</div><div id="48831582" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review"><meta content="Madden NFL 16" itemprop="itemReviewed"/><span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">Rated <span itemprop="ratingValue">9</span> out of <span itemprop="bestRating">10</span></span>\xc2\xa0by <span itemprop="author">Njbrown629</span><span itemprop="name"> It\'s...... Madden\n</span><span itemprop="description"> You can never expect Madden to change by leaps and bounds from year to year. I have purchased each one since 2004, and its just a simple fact. This years version is no different. I got it at its release date and started playing as soon as I could. The graphics are similar to the previous year, but the individual NFL stars do look more like themselves. The tackle animations seem less like animations and more like real momentum based impacts. The gains in XP and confidence per player (in franchise mode) make more sense with updates based on performance during the game instead of an ambiguous weekly gain. Overall I think it is a better game, and the improvements make it exciting while still being that same familiar game that I\'ve played for the past 11 years.\n</span> 8/27/15\n<meta content="2015-08-27" itemprop="datePublished"/>\n</div><div id="50163865" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review"><meta content="Madden NFL 16" itemprop="itemReviewed"/><span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">Rated <span itemprop="ratingValue">3</span> out of <span itemprop="bestRating">10</span></span>\xc2\xa0by <span itemprop="author">scoopd</span><span itemprop="name"> Blah\n</span><span itemprop="description"> The COD of sports games, next year comes, same as the last... I love sports and football, so naturally I buy Madden every year. I think with this iteration, I may have finally reached my limit. I defend Madden a lot because changing a football game is tough, but this year\'s Madden feels disturbingly similar to last year. Graphics and gameplay are the same as last year, decent if not above average. The presentation is mostly the same with some different stat overlays in-between plays and a few changes in what the announcers say. Disappointingly, the game modes are mostly untouched. The Gauntlet game type returns the same as last year, as does the Ultimate Team mode which once again offers micro transactions at every turn. Connected Franchise, which was mediocre last year, feels noticeably worse this year. The menus are incredibly slow and every feature outside of actual playing is hidden. It seemed the developers are trying to hide the fact that they didn\'t change anything by pushing all of the recycled content to the back of the pile of menus. Ranking up players, confidence, adjusting stadium prices, all seemingly left as is from last year. Sensing a theme? This years Madden just isn\'t good, it feels all too similar to last year with not enough new content to keep me playing. Outside of the people who play online a lot, I cannot recommend this game to anyone. There are better, more innovative titles coming out that require peoples attention.\n</span> 8/26/15\n<meta content="2015-08-26" itemprop="datePublished"/>\n</div><div id="50196813" itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review"><meta content="Madden NFL 16" itemprop="itemReviewed"/><span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">Rated <span itemprop="ratingValue">8</span> out of <span itemprop="bestRating">10</span></span>\xc2\xa0by <span itemprop="author">NYGiantsFan</span><span itemprop="name"> Good Game\n</span><span itemprop="description"> It is a great game like all games it could be better but it is very good for a yearly release.
